<Date>1574191067809</Date><text>I've seen a lot of reviews here about the complaints regarding the rent and its deeply concerning. Since I just moved in its hard for me to get a feel about the rent but I'm sure as time goes my my feelings may change.

As far as the amenities, I haven't used them that much. I noticed that they do have a pool, albeit small, and I've heard they had a jacuzzi. I noticed the laundry room and it was very small.

The park is pretty well clean, well kept and well maintained. The neighbors all seem quiet and the place is very quiet at night. Did I say the park looks clean? It sits on a hill so you do get an overlook of Glenview if you're lucky.

It's hard to recommend this place though because of the lack of amenities and the complaints of high rent. If they used the rent to put back into the community in the form of bigger pools, larger laundry rooms, an community center for residents, etc, I'd be more inclined to give it a higher rating.

Hopefully the rent doesn't drag this rating down because I do enjoy the peace and quiet, clean, friendly neighborhood.

Update November 2019: I've been here for a little over a month now. This is just an updated review on things.

I noticed that the community is well kept with Landscaping and maintenance. The maintenance guy always seems to be out repairing any faults in the community. And I've also seen contracted Landscaping here quite a bit. I'm very happy to see that management takes really good care of the community grounds.

The neighbors seem pretty friendly. And the community is very quiet. In fact I would highly recommend this community if you are looking for some sort of peace. The community is quiet during the day and also at night.

I haven't noticed any suspicious Behavior or trespassers in the community. I'm glad the community has a cul-de-sac sort of design. This community feels very quiet and very safe.

I have heard of equipment being stolen from someone's truck here. So you still can't leave all your belongings out in the open. Belongings and personal equipment are not totally safe as robberies still occur in this community.<//text>< user_id>

<username>Christopher Smith</username>< review>
5 Stars for the Awesome disc golf course in the park and natural wash. The 4 stars is for The park itself. The park hosts soft ball fields (2) and disc golf with a walking trail. No kids play equipment. No drinking water and only out houses. Small Parking lot 36 spaces is free and the gate is open at sunrise and closes sunset. Multiple tee pads and basket locations at each hole with seating at each tee. Beautiful place to play and very challenging. You can loose discs here and it's hard to figure out the course when your new. Murrieta Rattlers DGC maintains the course wonderfully and constantly with league and tournament play year round. The park needs water and restrooms for 5 stars. The parking lot overflows into the neiborhood during every organized event. If this was helpful please give me a like.<//review>

Love Trader Joe's, Dollar Tree and Simply Greek etc etc... The businesses are fantastic.. However the parking lot is beyond a nightmare. I purposely stay away unless it's in off hours. Today I came with my 8 yr old daughter. On our way out we were almost run over by a man and his wife in a minivan desperate for a close spot. He was not paying attention. I felt the wind and vibration from his van and I was behind my cart. My daughter who was on the side of the cart, had she been turned straight instead of sideways looking at me would have been hit. This man didn't care, refused to apologize, insisted he'd been there a long time. I was so flabbergasted. Two horrible lessons for my daughter to learn, 1) driving irresponsibly is ok and 2) you don't need to take responsibility when you are wrong. They definitely at the very least need cameras here and preferably a police presence who will stop these Mario Andretti drivers. So sad my day out with my girl ended like this. It's just wrong!!!</Text>
